Top 32 Decklists
================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX SEATTLE-TACOMA 2015](/en/events/coverage/gpsea15)
 on November 8, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











Already checked out the Top 8 decklists and need even more? These are the remaining Top 32 placing decklists, in ninth through thirty-second order, from Grand Prix Seattle-Tacoma!
